< Text>
Two Rivers RV Park

‚úÖ On the way to Yosemite always midway stop to park our RV on the San Joaquin river

‚úÖ Excellent riverside location for a family picnic. Grilling fish is my fave

‚úÖ Near great bass pro shop

‚úÖ Swim in river to end or start the day

‚úÖ New management, turnaround professionally ran, lots of upgrades in progress and pride is obvious.
Safe, very clean especially bathrooms, very reasonably priced

‚Äî‚Äî

We‚Äôve been coming in Two Rivers RV camp for many many years now both with our extended family and at times when I need a place for alone time to just camp, fish, swim, and relax. I love the setting, right on the San Joaquin River. My family and I have not had any issues with the people we‚Äôve met there and I made friends with some of the permanent guests which is probably one of the big reasons we return a couple of times a year. Fishing is my thing, the river is perfect for that and a well stocked pro shop is nearby.

I‚Äôm very pleasantly surprised with the changes I‚Äôve seen during my last trip, the parks  under new management and the change is like night and day, Things have been cleaned up, lots of painting going on, freshening up of the facilities, and the bathrooms have been attended to nicely.  I‚Äôve always felt safe here so that‚Äôs never been an issue but it‚Äôs clear that this is now a very well-maintained location, safe for the family, and the perfect getaway location. If you‚Äôre heading to Yosemite or nearby Manteca, definitely consider a stay here. Very reasonably priced compared to other parks in the state.< /Text>

I just bought a new RV and wanted to Camp local. The first time I went camping there the campsite host met us at the gate and collected money for three night stay and I told her we may stay at 4th night. The third day she comes running up right when I open my door at 7:30 in the morning saying we need to pay her for the next night. I told her I thought we already paid for three nights let me talk to my wife come back in an hour. Exactly one hour later she was knocking on our door. My wife told her that we had paid for three nights and we are not going to stay a fourth night and she argued with us for about 15 minutes and then when I told her I gave her the $100 bill and how much chain she gave me back she finally remembered. Then the second time we went there I brought my camper again and it was a holiday weekend so I got there Thursday night and my wife stayed home to go to work on Friday. So Friday my wife comes after work to drop off some groceries and beer in the lady tells her that she needs to pay a day use fee to be able to drop me off food if she's going to stay more than 5 minutes. So to avoid 2 days of overnight fees because she met me there I had to unhitch my truck from my trailer driving to town drop the car off at my house and come back to the campsite to avoid that extra $40 fee. The place was so much better when they didn't have this campsite host running it. I would give it to 0 Stars if I could.< /Text>

1.0 star rating3/16/2021
I purchased a prepaid device and plan from this T-Mobile location and it has turned into a HUGE headache. The staff is so poorly trained in T-Mobile operations I can't comprehend how they are allowed to take customers cash.

When I purchased the prepaid plan and asked about a receipt I was informed I would be emailed a receipt. I was never emailed a receipt. I have received no account information besides the phone number that was assigned to the device.

Before I purchased the device I was told by the three store employees who were present I had 30 days to return it (this is wrong, T-Mobile's policy is 14 days). The device didn't work out for me and I tried to return it with the store manager.

The store manager told me they can't do returns on prepaid devices, it is not possible. I was like what????

T-Mobiles policy on their website, the policy that came in the device's box, and your store employee all stated I could return the device within 14 days (well besides the employees who told me 30 days).

The store manager simply told me she couldn't process the return and to call customer support if I had a problem. At no point did it feel like the manager wanted to help resolve the situation.

I felt like I had been cheated and lied to. Everything says I should be able to return the device, and the manager basically tells me "no, it's not their problem, and to go find help somewhere else".

I called customer support multiple times and they all insisted the store should do the return. They said because the store processed the order wrong, and never gave me a receipt, I had to do the return in the store. I have no account information or anything, just a charge on my credit card.

When I went back into the store I explained the situation to the manager. They made a couple calls to other local T-Mobile stores and again repeated they can't do returns on prepaid devices.

My recourse now is to deal with T-Mobile's legal department who I've had to write a letter to (yes a letter, no email). What should have been a simple return has turned into a big time-wasting situation.

If you need to go to a T-Mobile I suggest finding a different location than this one.< /review>

<name>Thomas Carvalho</name>< review>
Took my 2016 Honda Civic here in 2019 because the AC stopped blowing cold while it was still under warranty. This was the second time it had happened which I told them.  First time was handled by another Honda dealer when I lived in another area.

I was told it was checked for leaks and while the freon was very low, there were no leaks. They refilled the Freon and performed a scheduled maintenance check.

A little over one year later my AC stopped blowing cold air again. I took it back to Marin Honda at which time they then found a leaky valve.

It is obvious that the leak had been there since I purchased the car as the freon had to be recharged every year but the leak was not detected the first time I took it to Marin Honda while under warranty.

They didn't own up to the fact that they missed it the previous time I took it in with the same problem and said it was a maintenance issue. I asked if the valve only lasts 1-3 years and got no answer.

Overall the gentleman that was working with me was pleasant, professional, and did try to help but they refused to own up to their mistake and I had to pay for it. I can't trust their service department and I will not be back.

*Update - The manager said to send my info and he would contact me to try to remedy. I sent my info. He never reached out. The dishonesty is worse than if they had just let it go. Can't trust this dealership.

AC is not working again after a year. Same thing as every spring. They never fixed it. There was a class action lawsuit which says there is a problem with the condenser for these cars. I'll take it to a different Honda dealer to see if they will agree to fix it under the extended warranty on these AC condensers. This dealership is not honest.< /review>

<review>(Owner asked me on this post to email him so I did and he hasn't responded. Clearly not interested in resolving only public image.)

We did not buy a car here so I can't comment on the purchasing process. My frustration comes with feeling like we were misled over the phone. I had been in contact with someone from their internet sales department (I won't mention their name out of respect for them) over a 2 day period. We live a 3 hour drive away but have a small flight that flys from our town to SF. We let the sales rep know that we would try to fly in on Sunday morning to look at the car. The night before the rep called me and said they would "set it aside and have it ready for us in the morning." We were not able to get on the first flight of the day and had to wait for the 2nd flight of the day for seats. I called at 9:30 before they opened and they confirmed, "We have it set aside and we are ready for you." When my wife arrived in SF they told us they had sold it while she was in the air!!

Then when we talked with them they said it's illegal to hold cars and they couldn't hold it. The rep even told me he said that before we left which i disagreed with and said I took, "We have set it aside and have it ready," to mean they were holding it. I would never have wanted them to break a law but rather to have been more up front and clear with what they meant with their statements before my wife and son boarded a flight to SF. They did offer us another car for what they said their lowest price would be as an apology but we didn't like the color enough to pay what they still wanted.

All of that to say I have learned that a dealer will not hold a car even if what they are saying sounds like they will, thats on me. My advice to Marin Honda is that you be more clear when you are talking with people who are going through great lengths to travel to your dealership to purchase a car from you. Clarity of communication is valuable and could have saved my family quite a bit of trouble today.< /review><pictures>None<//pictures>< Response>

<review>Today I experienced something to restore some of my (damaged) faith in human-kind:

My family bought a low-mileage certified Honda Insight from Marin five months ago. Marin received us late that day with tired children in tow, and stayed nearly two hours past regular closing time to complete our sale. The sales and financial people were sweet, courteous, and uncomplainingly worked overtime with us.

In those five months since, we put just over four-thousand miles on the car.
Last Sunday, I noticed that the front tires had prematurely and unevenly worn- to the point that they were nearly bald. Knowing this could be because of alignment or suspension, I called Marin. They asked me to bring it in the next day.

Here is where I fully expected to encounter baulking of some kind, and that I would have to argue the point of any misalignment as being responsible for the tire wear; in my head circulated tedious scenarios of letter-writing and explanation that I would have to undergo for some satisfaction, as the auto dealers I had encountered in the past fell under worse stereotypes of the profession.

Arriving at 9:30AM and explaining that I had to be back in the East Bay area to pick up my children from school, they prioritized my car. Still uneasy, I settled in the lounge with a free cappuccino and my book, thinking I would be there until the estimated 1:PM completion.
At 11:AM I was called to take my car.
They'd found and repaired the alignment issue and installed new tires at no charge to me. No argument, no hassle, pleasant, civilized, responsible, prompt- my God, what a relief! I'm so pleased- our experiences with Marin Honda have been some of the best we've had with any kind of business, ever.
Thanks, guys!< /review><pictures>None< /pictures><Resp>{'time': 1400889848943, 'text': 'Brian, Thank you for the positive review of our sales and service department!
